While comprehensive test coverage exists for happy path scenarios and basic error cases, several critical failure modes and edge cases in member state transitions, concurrent operations, and error recovery remain untested.\n\nThis analysis identifies 5+ specific test coverage gaps that could lead to production issues, particularly around:\n- Concurrent member epoch conflicts during rapid state changes\n- Incomplete partition revocation during member re-joins\n- Metadata refresh failures during group rebalancing\n- Static member fencing grace period boundary conditions\n- Share/Streams group state mutation race conditions\n\n---\n\n## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Concurrent Member Epoch Conflict During Rapid Heartbeats with State Changes\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 2299-2465 (consumerGroupHeartbeat method), ~lines 1562-1584 (throwIfConsumerGroupMemberEpochIsInvalid)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a member submits heartbeats with conflicting epochs (e.g., member resubmits epoch N while coordinator has already advanced to N+1), the current validation logic at line 1571-1583 only accepts the member if it has epoch N or N-1. However, the test suite does not comprehensively cover the scenario where:\n1. Member sends heartbeat with epoch N and gets response with epoch N+1\n2. Member re-sends the previous heartbeat with epoch N before processing the N+1 response (due to network jitter or client bug)\n3. Coordinator receives both requests in sequence\n\nThe edge case is that the `previousMemberEpoch()` tracking may not be set correctly if multiple concurrent updates happen, potentially leading to FencedMemberEpochException in valid recovery scenarios or accepting invalid epoch conflicts.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testConcurrentMemberEpochConflictDuringRapidHeartbeats() context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(createHeartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId, 0));\n    assertEquals(1, result1.response().memberEpoch());\n\n    // Send heartbeat with epoch 1 -> gets epoch 2\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result2 =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(createHeartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId, 1));\n    assertEquals(2, result2.response().memberEpoch());\n\n    // Simulate network jitter: resend epoch 1 request before epoch 2 is processed\n    // This should be rejected or handled gracefully, not cause state Member A acknowledges revocation but hasn't yet released the partitions\n3. Before partition release is confirmed, Member A sends a new heartbeat requesting to rejoin with epoch 0\n4. The coordinator should properly reset the member's state and clear pending revocations\n\nThe edge case is that the `maybeReconcile()` method (around line 2432) may not properly handle the transition The resolution fails mid-operation (e.g., metadata update times out)\n4. When a static member with instance ID is marked with epoch -2, the coordinator allows the same instance ID to be reassigned only after a grace period (session timeout).\n\nThe test suite has tests for this behavior, but lacks coverage for exact boundary conditions:\n1. Static member A with instance ID \"inst-1\" leaves with epoch -2 at time T\n2. New member B tries to join with same instance ID \"inst-1\" at time T + (session_timeout - 1ms)\n3. The coordinator should reject with `UNRELEASED_INSTANCE_ID`\n4. At time T + (session_timeout + 1ms), member B should be allowed to join\n\nThe edge case is in the timing logic around when the grace period expires. The current code at line 1628 checks if `memberEpoch() != LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH`, but this doesn't account for the timeout grace period expiration.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testStaticMemberFencingGracePeriodBoundary() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String instanceId = \"instance-1\";\n    String member1Id = context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n        .build();\n\n    // Member 1 joins with static instance ID\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(member1Id)\n            .setMemberEpoch(0)\n            .setInstanceId(instanceId)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(60000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\"))\n            .setTopicPartitions(List.of()));\n\n    long currentTime = context.time().milliseconds();\n\n    // Member 1 leaves with static member epoch -2\n    result = context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n        .setGroupId(groupId)\n        .setMemberId(member1Id)\n        .setMemberEpoch(LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH)\n        .setInstanceId(instanceId));\n\n    // Immediately try to join with different member ID and same instance ID\n    // Should be rejected because grace period hasn't expired\n    assertThrows(UnreleasedInstanceIdException.class, () ->\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(member2Id)\n            .setMemberEpoch(0)\n            .setInstanceId(instanceId)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(60000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\"))\n            .setTopicPartitions(List.of()))\n    );\n\n    // Advance time to just before grace period expires\n    int sessionTimeoutMs = 45000; // Default consumer group session timeout\n    context.sleep(sessionTimeoutMs - 1);\n\n    // Still should be rejected (1ms before grace period)\n    assertThrows(UnreleasedInstanceIdException.class, () ->\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(member2Id)\n            .setMemberEpoch(0)\n            .setInstanceId(instanceId)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(60000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\"))\n            .setTopicPartitions(List.of()))\n    );\n\n    // Advance time past grace period\n    context.sleep(2); // Total: sessionTimeoutMs + 1\n\n    // Now should be allowed to join with different member ID\n    result = context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n        .setGroupId(groupId)\n        .setMemberId(member2Id)\n        .setMemberEpoch(0)\n        .setInstanceId(instanceId)\n        .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(60000)\n        .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\"))\n        .setTopicPartitions(List.of()));\n\n    assertEquals(1, result.response().memberEpoch());\n    assertEquals(member2Id, result.response().memberId());\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**: This test would exercise:\n- Exact timing of the grace period expiration in static member fencing\n- Boundary condition at `session_timeout - 1ms` and `session_timeout + 1ms`\n- Integration of session timeout and fencing grace period\n- Verification of `throwIfInstanceIdIsUnreleased()` logic (line 1627-1635)\n- State cleanup after grace period expires\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 5: Share Group Concurrent State Mutation During Partition Assignment Update\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4932-5100 (shareGroupHeartbeat), ~lines 3573-3750 (handling share group partition assignments), ~lines 4270-4310 (shareGroupFenceMember)\n\n**Description**:\nShare groups support concurrent state updates during partition assignment. The coordinator maintains:\n- `currentAssignment`: the member's current partition assignment\n- `targetAssignment`: the desired state for the member\n- `partitionsPendingRevocation`: partitions waiting to be released\n\nThe test suite covers basic scenarios but lacks coverage for this edge case:\n1. Share group member M1 is assigned partitions [0,1,2]\n2. Target assignment changes to [1,2,3] (0 removed, 3 added)\n3. Member M1 sends heartbeat acknowledging revocation of [0] but release incomplete\n4. A concurrent metadata update happens that affects partition 2\n5. The coordinator processes both the member heartbeat and metadata update simultaneously\n\nThe edge case is in `shareGroupHeartbeat()` method and how it interacts with concurrent metadata mutations. Lines 3573-3750 and 4270-4310 handle share group state updates but may not properly serialize concurrent updates.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void .setMemberId(memberId)\n            .setMemberEpoch(0)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(60000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"share-topic\")));\n\n    int memberEpoch =
